2014/11/16 04:13:29	 	  creating trigger au_last_upload sql: create trigger au_last_upload 
 after update on last_upload 
 for each row  
 begin 
 	set @from_date=old.updated_on; 
 	set @to_date=new.updated_on; 
 	set @created_by=old.created_by; 
 	IF (CHAR_LENGTH(@from_date) = 0) THEN  
      SET @from_date = (now() - INTERVAL 20 YEAR); 
     END IF; 
     IF (CHAR_LENGTH(@created_by) = 8) THEN  CREATE TEMPORARY TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `temp_inclusion_list3t` (`root_vendor_article_id` int(11) default '0', `visible_master_vendor_article_id` int(11) default '0',  `quantity` int(11) NULL default NULL, `visible_quantity` int(11) NULL default NULL, `clsfn_override_quantity` int(11) NULL default NULL, `reserved_quantity` int(11) NULL default NULL, PRIMARY KEY  (`visible_master_vendor_article_id`,`root_vendor_article_id`) );insert into temp_inclusion_list3t (`root_vendor_article_id`, `visible_master_vendor_article_id` ,`quantity`, `visible_quantity`,`clsfn_override_quantity` ,`reserved_quantity`)
 select distinct root_vendor_article_id, visible_master_vendor_article_id, 
  sum(case when a.article_type_domain_id in (1013,1015) or va.order_type_domain_id = 5051 then 999 else case when va.quantity is null then 0 else va.quantity end end), 
  sum(case when va.order_type_domain_id = 5056 then 999 else case when va.quantity is null then 0 else va.quantity end end), 
  coalesce((select max(case when vac9.override_quantity is null then 0 else vac9.override_quantity end) from vendor_article_clsfn vac9  where vac9.vendor_article_id2 = mai.vendor_article_id) ,0), 
  coalesce((select sum(case when adj.quantity is null then 0 else adj.quantity end) from vendor_article_stock_adj adj inner join master_article_index mai9c on mai9c.vendor_article_id = adj.vendor_article_id where mai9c.visible_master_vendor_article_id = mai.visible_master_vendor_article_id),0) 
 from master_article_index mai inner join vendor_article va on va.vendor_article_id = mai.vendor_article_id 
 and va.updated_on >= @from_date and va.updated_on <= @to_date  inner join article a on a.article_id = va.article_id 
 where visible_master_vendor_article_id is not null 
 group by root_vendor_article_id, visible_master_vendor_article_id ;INSERT INTO master_article_index (vendor_article_id,root_vendor_article_id,created_by,cache_visible_quantity, cache_quantity, cache_reserved_quantity) 
 select distinct mai.vendor_article_id, mai.root_vendor_article_id, 'websiteupd',  
 case when a.article_type_domain_id in (1013,1015) or va.order_type_domain_id in (5051,5056) then 999 else 
  case when mai.cache_is_visible_as_listing = 0 and mai.cache_is_leaf = 1 and a.article_type_domain_id = 1016 then 
   case when va.quantity is null then 0 else va.quantity - til3.clsfn_override_quantity + til3.reserved_quantity end  
  else  
   til3.quantity - til3.clsfn_override_quantity + til3.reserved_quantity 
  end 
 end, 
 case when va.order_type_domain_id = 5056 then 999 else 
  case when mai.cache_is_visible_as_listing = 0 and mai.cache_is_leaf = 1 and a.article_type_domain_id = 1016 then 
   case when va.quantity is null then 0 else va.quantity - til3.clsfn_override_quantity + til3.reserved_quantity end  
  else  
   case when til3.visible_quantity is null then 0 else til3.visible_quantity - til3.clsfn_override_quantity + til3.reserved_quantity end 
  end 
 end, 
 til3.reserved_quantity 
 from vendor_article_clsfn vac inner join vendor_article va on va.vendor_article_id = vac.vendor_article_id2  inner join master_article_index mai on mai.vendor_article_id = va.vendor_article_id inner join temp_inclusion_list3t til3 on til3.root_vendor_article_id = mai.root_vendor_article_id and til3.visible_master_vendor_article_id = mai.visible_master_vendor_article_id inner join article a on a.article_id = va.article_id 
 where va.updated_on >= @from_date and va.updated_on <= @to_date 
 FOR UPDATE 
 ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE cache_visible_quantity=VALUES(cache_visible_quantity), cache_quantity=VALUES(cache_quantity), cache_reserved_quantity=VALUES(cache_reserved_quantity) ;

 INSERT INTO master_list_class_index (root_vendor_article_id, list_class_clsfn_domain_id, list_class_type_domain_id, list_class_hdr_id, list_class_id, description, member_count, visible_member_count)  
 select 
  mai.root_vendor_article_id, 
  lcc.list_class_clsfn_domain_id,  lcc.list_class_type_domain_id , lc.list_class_hdr_id, 
  lc.list_class_id, lc.description, count(distinct mai.visible_master_vendor_article_id), 
  count(distinct case when mai.cache_visible_quantity > 0 then mai.visible_master_vendor_article_id else null end) 
  from list_class lc 
  inner join list_class_clsfn lcc on lcc.list_class_id = lc.list_class_id 
  inner join master_article_index mai on mai.vendor_article_id = lcc.object_id 
  inner join vendor_article va on va.vendor_article_id = lcc.object_id inner join article a on a.article_id = va.article_id 
  group by lcc.list_class_clsfn_domain_id,  lcc.list_class_type_domain_id , lc.list_class_hdr_id, lc.list_class_id, lc.description 
  FOR UPDATE 
  ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE description=VALUES(description), member_count=VALUES(member_count), visible_member_count=VALUES(visible_member_count) ;
     END IF; 
 end
